\"pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go\", \"symbol\": \"Hook\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"API key authentication in Grafana is implemented across several files:\\n\\n1. **pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go** — The primary API key authentication client. The `APIKey` struct implements `authn.ContextAwareClient` and `authn.HookClient`. The `Authenticate` method extracts the token from the HTTP `Authorization` header (Bearer or Basic with username `api_key`), looks it up via the apikey service, and calls `validateApiKey` to enforce key validity. `validateApiKey` checks: (a) key expiration (`errAPIKeyExpired`), (b) revocation status (`errAPIKeyRevoked`), (c) organization mismatch (`errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`), and (d) that the key is linked to a service account (plain API keys without service accounts are rejected as `errAPIKeyInvalid`). The `Hook` method asynchronously updates `last_used_at` after successful auth. Both legacy (HMAC-based) and modern (satokengen-prefixed) token formats are supported via `getFromTokenLegacy` and `getFromToken`.\\n\\n2. **pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go** — The HTTP middleware (`ContextHandler.Middleware`) that initializes the request context. It calls `h.authenticator.Authenticate`, which dispatches to the registered authn clients (including `APIKey`). On success, the signed-in user is placed in the context. The handler also tracks auth HTTP headers (`Authorization`) used for API keys.\\n\\n3. **pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go** — The `Service` interface defining CRUD operations for API keys: `GetAllAPIKeys`, `AddAPIKey`, `GetApiKeyByName`, `GetAPIKeyByHash`, `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate`.\\n\\n4. **pkg/services/apikey/model.go** — The `APIKey` struct (DB model) with fields: `ID`, `OrgID`, `Name`, `Key` (hash), `Role`, `Created`, `Updated`, `LastUsedAt`, `Expires` (expiration timestamp pointer for expiry enforcement), `ServiceAccountId`, `IsRevoked`.\\n\\n5. **pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go** — The concrete `Service` implementation backed by SQL. `GetAPIKeyByHash` and `GetApiKeyByName` retrieve keys from the DB; `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate` updates the `last_used_at` field.\\n\\n6. **pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go** — SQL store implementation. `GetAPIKeyByHash` looks up by hashed key value. `AddAPIKey` creates keys with expiry. `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate` records last usage.\\n\\n7. **pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/store.go** — Internal store interface used by the service implementation.\\n\\n8. **pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go** — gRPC-layer API key authentication. The `authenticator.getSignedInUser` method validates a Bearer token by hash, fetches the associated service account, enforces `org.RoleAdmin` role requirement (scope enforcement for gRPC), and checks that the service account is not disabled. Permissions are loaded via `AccessControlService.GetUserPermissions`.\\n\\n9. **pkg/services/authn/authn.go** — Defines `ClientAPIKey = \\\"auth.client.api-key\\\"` constant and the `authn.Request`/`authn.Identity` types used throughout the auth flow.\\n\\n10. **pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go** — Registers the `APIKey` client with the authn service via `authnSvc.RegisterClient(clients.ProvideAPIKey(apikeyService, tracer))`.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
